## CgratesWebJsonapiWeb.LoadTariffPlanController
### CgratesWebJsonapiWeb.LoadTariffPlanController.create
#### executes LoadTariffPlanFromStorDb when data is valid
##### Request
* __Method:__ POST
* __Path:__ /api/load-tariff-plan
* __Request headers:__
```
accept: application/vnd.api+json
content-type: application/vnd.api+json
authorization: bearer: eyJhbGciOiJIUzUxMiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJhdWQiOiJjZ3JhdGVzX3dlYl9qc29uYXBpIiwiZXhwIjoxNjA4NTY3NTA0LCJpYXQiOjE2MDYxNDgzMDQsImlzcyI6ImNncmF0ZXNfd2ViX2pzb25hcGkiLCJqdGkiOiIwMmFjMzFmZS1jNzA4LTQ0ZDUtOWIwZC03ZWIwZWZiNDRiYWEiLCJuYmYiOjE2MDYxNDgzMDMsInN1YiI6IjM5OSIsInR5cCI6ImFjY2VzcyJ9.XkNN3N5kmIcWB3fkLClFcYPy0U8K_ZPYRbmR2LIaIcgn94u8E-o6-zbeVjyFSUEqnvASZP35inXO5T3ZZ9iZ5w
```
* __Request body:__
```json
{
  "meta": {},
  "data": {
    "attributes": {
      "validate": true,
      "tpid": "tp",
      "flush-db": false,
      "dry-run": false
    }
  }
}
```
##### Response
* __Status__: 201
* __Response headers:__
```
content-type: application/json; charset=utf-8
cache-control: max-age=0, private, must-revalidate
x-request-id: FkovX3ErXQgl24wAAE2K
vary: Origin
access-control-allow-origin: *
access-control-expose-headers: 
access-control-allow-credentials: true
```
* __Response body:__
```json
{
  "result": "OK",
  "id": null,
  "error": null
}
```

## CgratesWebJsonapiWeb.TpActionPlanController
### CgratesWebJsonapiWeb.TpActionPlanController.create
#### POST create does not create resource and renders errors when data is invalid
##### Request
* __Method:__ POST
* __Path:__ /api/tp-action-plans
* __Request headers:__
```
accept: application/vnd.api+json
content-type: application/vnd.api+json
authorization: bearer: eyJhbGciOiJIUzUxMiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJhdWQiOiJjZ3JhdGVzX3dlYl9qc29uYXBpIiwiZXhwIjoxNjA4NTY3NTAwLCJpYXQiOjE2MDYxNDgzMDAsImlzcyI6ImNncmF0ZXNfd2ViX2pzb25hcGkiLCJqdGkiOiJlODA3ZTQ5NS0zM2Y1LTQ4MzMtYWFjMC1jODRmZDEwZjJiYWMiLCJuYmYiOjE2MDYxNDgyOTksInN1YiI6IjMyMyIsInR5cCI6ImFjY2VzcyJ9.HFx1P2DRzya77rYBWV5q9MT1QK3gnff6k4nV1KLxBPfcjLlVoOTSu7BOomd7EdDDUDyIFqkYF5bZa98HGBLTjg
```
* __Request body:__
```json
{
  "meta": {},
  "data": {
    "type": "tp_action_plan",
    "attributes": {
      "tag": null
    }
  }
}
```
##### Response
* __Status__: 422
* __Response headers:__
```
content-type: application/vnd.api+json; charset=utf-8
cache-control: max-age=0, private, must-revalidate
x-request-id: FkovXrkBz1BsaZ4AAKAB
vary: Origin
access-control-allow-origin: *
access-control-expose-headers: 
access-control-allow-credentials: true
```
* __Response body:__
```json
{
  "jsonapi": {
    "version": "1.0"
  },
  "errors": [
    {
      "title": "can't be blank",
      "source": {
        "pointer": "/data/attributes/tpid"
      },
      "detail": "Tpid can't be blank"
    },
    {
      "title": "can't be blank",
      "source": {
        "pointer": "/data/attributes/tag"
      },
      "detail": "Tag can't be blank"
    },
    {
      "title": "can't be blank",
      "source": {
        "pointer": "/data/attributes/actions-tag"
      },
      "detail": "Actions tag can't be blank"
    },
    {
      "title": "can't be blank",
      "source": {
        "pointer": "/data/attributes/timing-tag"
      },
      "detail": "Timing tag can't be blank"
    },
    {
      "title": "can't be blank",
      "source": {
        "pointer": "/data/attributes/weight"
      },
      "detail": "Weight can't be blank"
    }
  ]
}
```

#### POST create creates and renders resource when data is valid
##### Request
* __Method:__ POST
* __Path:__ /api/tp-action-plans
* __Request headers:__
```
accept: application/vnd.api+json
content-type: application/vnd.api+json
authorization: bearer: eyJhbGciOiJIUzUxMiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJhdWQiOiJjZ3JhdGVzX3dlYl9qc29uYXBpIiwiZXhwIjoxNjA4NTY3NTAxLCJpYXQiOjE2MDYxNDgzMDEsImlzcyI6ImNncmF0ZXNfd2ViX2pzb25hcGkiLCJqdGkiOiI1ZjU2ODI0NC1lOWQwLTQ0MWQtODE5OC1lYWViZGQ5OTI3ZTkiLCJuYmYiOjE2MDYxNDgzMDAsInN1YiI6IjMzMSIsInR5cCI6ImFjY2VzcyJ9.LDGReQ2LAY89Th8MPPGj4mKtc5TepbclqVB4UH1WLuhDOI3UBIqGlyNTgyZv7nOw_XAXdA4uGEeocYJK1WrBxg
```
* __Request body:__
```json
{
  "meta": {},
  "data": {
    "type": "tp_action_plan",
    "attributes": {
      "weight": 10.0,
      "tpid": "82cf74f0-36a3-4ef4-88a2-6662ec172724",
      "timing_tag": "58fbb53d-9488-4bc5-9a81-bb541deaea9f",
      "tag": "49eb11d8-d7b4-4a34-b50f-a14cbd2e734a",
      "actions_tag": "670839b3-37ff-4090-b29e-78eda078bf9e"
    }
  }
}
```
##### Response
* __Status__: 201
* __Response headers:__
```
content-type: application/vnd.api+json; charset=utf-8
cache-control: max-age=0, private, must-revalidate
x-request-id: FkovXrqHBAhyCnUAAKQB
vary: Origin
access-control-allow-origin: *
access-control-expose-headers: 
access-control-allow-credentials: true
```
* __Response body:__
```json
{
  "jsonapi": {
    "version": "1.0"
  },
  "data": {
    "type": "tp-action-plan",
    "id": "20",
    "attributes": {
      "weight": "10.0",
      "tpid": "82cf74f0-36a3-4ef4-88a2-6662ec172724",
      "timing-tag": "58fbb53d-9488-4bc5-9a81-bb541deaea9f",
      "tag": "49eb11d8-d7b4-4a34-b50f-a14cbd2e734a",
      "created-at": null,
      "actions-tag": "670839b3-37ff-4090-b29e-78eda078bf9e"
    }
  }
}
```

### CgratesWebJsonapiWeb.TpActionPlanController.export_to_csv

* __Method:__ GET
* __Path:__ /api/tp-action-plans/export-to-csv?filter[actions_tag]=at1&filter[timing_tag]=t1&tpid=f4424cff-8e26-4fa2-b15f-7127b9b2eb5c
* __Request headers:__
```
accept: application/vnd.api+json
content-type: application/vnd.api+json
authorization: bearer: eyJhbGciOiJIUzUxMiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJhdWQiOiJjZ3JhdGVzX3dlYl9qc29uYXBpIiwiZXhwIjoxNjA4NTY3NTAwLCJpYXQiOjE2MDYxNDgzMDAsImlzcyI6ImNncmF0ZXNfd2ViX2pzb25hcGkiLCJqdGkiOiI0MTU2YWMyZC01NmYwLTQxYTgtOGVkMi05YzE2ZGNhYzk3YmUiLCJuYmYiOjE2MDYxNDgyOTksInN1YiI6IjMyMCIsInR5cCI6ImFjY2VzcyJ9.CSBG77cV2on8DLJVG0M_1KYYwZz3zft7l0dbjTXDM0f1Qhho_zRLOVUzXi8kq9WP0ScObDl2fgDQnyOdQc8CVw
```
##### Response
* __Status__: 200
* __Response headers:__
```
cache-control: max-age=0, private, must-revalidate

vary: Origin
access-control-allow-origin: *
```

### CgratesWebJsonapiWeb.TpActionPlanController.index
#### GET index filtering by weight
